	To try and determine if the actual values of constants and coefficients 
matter to a student solving a problem, I have compared the results of all 
steps with the same format but different values.  The first line in these 
results is the format of the equation i.e. the equation with arbitrary values.  
The next lines are the times that the student wrote a correct input given the 
equation seen to the right.
	The idea behind this was that student performance on a step with a certain 
format should be similar across all instances of that format (different 
values, same format) if that actual values don’t matter regarding student 
performance.
